\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortrancode_8l_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{ * For fixed formatted code position 6 is of importance (continuation character).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortrancode_8l_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{ * The following variables and macros keep track of the column number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortrancode_8l_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{ * YY\_USER\_ACTION is always called for each scan action}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortrancode_8l_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{ * YY\_FTN\_RESET   is used to handle end of lines and reset the column counter}}
